            if ( MathCompare(&evt_VALOR_F4311_2,&mnLocal384)<0 )

               VA evt_UPMJ_2 is less than or equal to BF DataFinal */

                (LPVOID)&lpDS->DataInicial,EVDT_JDEDATE)>=0 &&

  if ( lpDS->Executado==cLocal538 )

    /* VA evt_TOT_LIVROS = "1" */
    ParseNumericStringEx( &evt_TOT_LIVROS ,
        _J("1") , DEFAULT_SEPARATOR | CURRENCY_KEEP );

    /* IF BF Livro2 is greater than <Blank> */
    if ( jdestrcmpwithnull(lpDS->Livro2,szLocal539)>0 )
    {

      /* VA evt_TOT_LIVROS = "2" */
      ParseNumericStringEx( &evt_TOT_LIVROS ,
          _J("2") , DEFAULT_SEPARATOR | CURRENCY_KEEP );

    ParseNumericStringEx( &evt_CONT ,
        _J("1") , DEFAULT_SEPARATOR | CURRENCY_KEEP );

    /* WHILE VA evt_CONT is less than or equal to VA evt_TOT_LIVROS */
    while ( MathCompare(&evt_CONT,&evt_TOT_LIVROS)<=0 )
    {

      /* IF VA evt_CONT is equal to "1" */
      if ( MathCompare(&evt_CONT,&mnLocal540)==0 )
      {

            DIM( evt_LT ) );

      {

        /* VA evt_LT = BF Livro2 */

            DIM( evt_LT ) );

      /* IF BF PNInicial is equal to BF PNFinal */
      if ( MathCompare(&lpDS->PNInicial,&lpDS->PNFinal)==0 )
      {

        /* IF VA evt_OBJ_SUBI is not equal to VA evt_OBJ_SUBF */

        {

          /* V550911PF.Select */

              _J("V550911PF") , 13L , 1 , &hReqV550911PF );

            {

              zSelect541[0].Item1.idInstance = 0L;
              zSelect541[0].lpValue = (LPVOID)evt_SINAL;
              zSelect541[0].nCmp = JDEDB_CMP_GT;
              jdeNIDcpy( zSelect541[1].Item1.szDict , _J("DGJ") );
              jdeNIDcpy( zSelect541[1].Item1.szTable , _J("F0911") );
              zSelect541[1].Item1.idInstance = 0L;
              zSelect541[1].lpValue = (LPVOID)&lpDS->DataInicial;

  if ( pszLocal554 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal554 ); }
  if ( pszLocal557 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal557 ); }
  if ( pszLocal558 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal558 ); }
  if ( pszLocal559 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal559 ); }
  if ( pszLocal560 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal560 ); }
  if ( pszLocal580 ) { jdeFree( pszLocal580 ); }
  if ( hUser ) { JDB_FreeBhvr( hUser ); }

  return idRtnVal;

} /* end of InvestimentoEconomico */
